Import Libraries

  • Request library allows you to send HTTP request in python to a specific URL. In our case we send an HTTP request to Zillow
  • Time module allows to handle time related task including formatting dates, waiting and representing time
  • The random module allows you to generate random
  • The bs4 module allows you to pull data from HTML document after you get a response from HTTP request
  • The os modules allows ou to interact with operating systems including changing working directory
  • The selenium module allows you to automate interaction with a web browser including sending URL request and extracting HTML document response
import requests
import time
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
from random import sample 
import pandas as pd 
import os
from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.chrome.options import Options
import json
import csv
from datetime import datetime
import re
from selenium_stealth import stealth

Set Path

  • Identify your destination folder
  • Use os change directory to set your destination directory as the default. That is where all outputs will be exported to
path = "../webscraping_outputs-Z"
os.chdir(path)

Create a file name

  • Create an outfile file name, I called mine ZillowSelium and formatted it a date time stamp
  • Note: If you are scraping multiple times in a day, then you need to format the time stamp with hours that way you don’t overwrite already exported data
finalfile = "ZillowSelenium" + "_" + "{:%Y_%h_%d_%H-%M-%S}".format(datetime.now()) +".csv"
finalfile
'ZillowSelenium_2023_Dec_10_19-09-38.csv'

Main Webscraping

  • Output results
  • Page numbers
  • URL
  • Selenium Setup
def getRealtorLinks(bases=["https://www.zillow.com/philadelphia-pa/rentals/","https://www.zillow.com/philadelphia-pa/for_sale/"], 
                    driver=webdriver.Chrome()):

    page_links = []
    linkSelector = "div.StyledPropertyCardDataWrapper-c11n-8-84-3__sc-1omp4c3-0"
    
    for url in bases:
        driver.get(url)
        html = driver.execute_script("return document.documentElement.outerHTML")
        soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')

        for item in soup.select(linkSelector):
            l = item.select("a")[0].attrs["href"]
            if not(l.startswith("https://")):
                l = "https://www.zillow.com"+l
            page_links.append(l)

        print(page_links[-1])

    return page_links


def getDesc(page_links, driver):

    titleSelector = "h1.Text-c11n-8-84-3__sc-aiai24-0"
    descSelector = "div.building-description"
    saleSelector = "div.Text-c11n-8-84-3__sc-aiai24-0"
    sale2Selector = "p.Text-c11n-8-84-3__sc-aiai24-0"
    nhoodSelector = "h2.styledComponents__BuildingCardTitle-sc-1bj2ydz-8"

    checkPhrases = ["This property accepts Zillow applications.","Zillow last checked"]

    entry = []

    for i in range(len(page_links)):

        ovPage = driver.get(page_links[i])
        textSoup = BeautifulSoup(driver.page_source,"html.parser")
        title = textSoup.select(titleSelector)[0].text
        desc1 = textSoup.select(descSelector)
        desc2 = textSoup.select(sale2Selector)
        desc3 = textSoup.select(saleSelector)

        elements = textSoup.select(nhoodSelector)
        nhood = None
        for e in elements:
            # print(e.text.lower)
            if "neighborhood" in e.text.lower():
                nhood = e.text.split(": ")[1]
                break
        


        if len(desc1)>0 and len(desc1[0].text)>70 and not(any(phrase in desc1 for phrase in checkPhrases)):
            text = desc1[0].text
        elif len(desc2)>0 and len(desc2[0].text)>70 and not(any(phrase in desc2 for phrase in checkPhrases)):
            text= desc2[0].text
        elif len(desc3)>0 and len(desc3[0].text)>70 and not(any(phrase in desc3 for phrase in checkPhrases)):
            text= desc3[0].text
        else:
            text=""

        entry.append({
            "title": title,
            "neighborhood": nhood,
            "description": text,
            "url": page_links[i]
        })
        
        print(f"title: {title}\nneighborhood: {nhood}\nlink: {page_links[i]}\n\n\t{text}\n\n")
        time.sleep(1)
    
    return entry
#Create a list that will hold the results

results = []

url_rent ="https://www.zillow.com/philadelphia-pa/rentals/"

url_sale = "https://www.zillow.com/philadelphia-pa/for_sale/"

options = webdriver.ChromeOptions()
# options.add_argument("start-maximized")

# options.add_argument("--headless")

# options.add_experimental_option("excludeSwitches", ["enable-automation"])
# options.add_experimental_option('useAutomationExtension', False)
driver = webdriver.Chrome(options=options)
textDriver = webdriver.Chrome(options=options)

stealth(driver,
        languages=["en-US", "en"],
        vendor="Google Inc.",
        platform="Win32",
        webgl_vendor="Intel Inc.",
        renderer="Intel Iris OpenGL Engine",
        fix_hairline=True,
        )

stealth(textDriver,
        languages=["en-US", "en"],
        vendor="Google Inc.",
        platform="Win32",
        webgl_vendor="Intel Inc.",
        renderer="Intel Iris OpenGL Engine",
        fix_hairline=True,
        )

# Inspect the zillow website and figure out the number pages for rental ads use
# In the charlotte example, there are a total of 20 pages so I set the range at 21

for page in range(1,21,1):
    
    print("This is page: " + str(page))
    
    #Identify the Zillow URL of your City, it should follow this format:
    # 1. Default Zillow url : https://www.zillow.com/
    # 2. Name of your City: eg. charlotte-nc, atlanta-ga
    # 3. Pass the page number 
    # 4. Add the "_p" that is a default thing with the Zillow website 
    # 5. In a sample URL on page 15 for example will be like: https://www.zillow.com/charlotte-nc/rentals/15_p/

    page = str(page) + '_p/'

    # CraiglistBrowser.maximize_window()

    # After the browser has been launched use the get() to pass the url 
    # print(f"Urls:\n")
    
    if len(results)>0:
        results.extend(getDesc(getRealtorLinks([url_rent+page,url_sale+page],driver=driver),driver=textDriver))
    else:
        results = getDesc(getRealtorLinks([url_rent+page,url_sale+page],driver=driver),driver=textDriver)


    time.sleep(0.5)

Zillowdata =  pd.DataFrame(results)
Zillowdata.to_csv(finalfile, index = False)

Geocoding with OpenStreetMaps API (Free)

import urllib
import requests

data = "Robin Apartments, 2003 Chestnut St, Philadelphia, PA 19103"

text = data
for word in range(len(text)):
    if text[word].isnumeric():
        address = text[word:]
        break

url = 'https://nominatim.openstreetmap.org/search?q=' + urllib.parse.quote(address) +'?format=json'
print(url)
response = requests.get(url)
coordSoup = BeautifulSoup(response.content,"html.parser")
print(response.content)
coordSoup.select("title")
'''

Manually Make CSVs

  1. run the first block to get the urls for either rental or for_sale listings
    • if you want both, repeat from step 4 or change code to use both urls (driver.get(other_url) and for loop or repeat code below)
  2. Recreate the driver with the next block
  3. Initialize the results list with the results = [] block
  4. run the for loop
    • as the webpages load in, press the read more or show more buttons to ensure all text is grabbed
  5. continue to finalfile code block and check created csv

if method==1:
    for item in soup.select(linkSelector):

        page_links.append(l)

    # results = []
    page_links

for i in range(len(page_links)):

    link=page_links[i]
    ovPage = driver.get(link)
    textSoup = BeautifulSoup(driver.page_source,"html.parser")
    title = textSoup.select(titleSelector)[0].text

    if len(textSoup.select(descSelector))>0 and len(textSoup.select(descSelector)[0].text)>70:
        text = textSoup.select(descSelector)[0].text
    elif len(textSoup.select(sale2Selector)[0]) and len(textSoup.select(sale2Selector)[0].text)>70:
        text= textSoup.select(sale2Selector)[0].text
    elif len(textSoup.select(saleSelector)[0])>0 and len(textSoup.select(saleSelector)[0].text)>70:
        text= textSoup.select(saleSelector)[0].text
    else:
        text=""

    results.append({
        "title": title,
        "description": text,
        "url": link
    })
    print(f"title: {title}\nlink: {link}\n\n\t{text}\n\n")
    time.sleep(3)

results = []
for link in page_links:
    ovPage = textDriver.get(link)
    textSoup = BeautifulSoup(textDriver.page_source,"html.parser")

    if len(textSoup.select("div.px-captcha-container")) > 0:
        time.sleep(3)
        continue
    else:
    
        title = textSoup.select(titleSelector)[0].text
        text = textSoup.select(descSelector)[0].text

        results.append({
            "title": title,
            "description": text,
            "url": link
        })
        print(f"title: {title}\nlink{link}")

    time.sleep(3)
    print(textDriver.getWebHandle())

textDriver.quit()
